Is it okay place. I've been coming here for 20 years, since they opened as Chico Self Serve.

They try to keep their prices comparable with eBay and AutoZone now days on a lot of things.

God forbid you take off your muzzle when you are at least 50 feet away from the nearest person.

I went in there a couple weeks ago. When I got out to the yard and away from anybody else, I had the audacity to lower my mask.

This shrill sounding Karen came running out to the yard hollering at people "SIR,  I need you to put on your mask!!", even if they were 50 feet away from anybody else.

She even saw some people underneath of vehicle working.  She went to the vehicle,  crouched down to do a mask check,  got right into their face within 4 feet and demanded that they put their masks on, breaking social distancing rules.

This mask policy has been selectively enforced. I have seen employees walking out to the yard without a mask on and nothing was said.

I also noticed that this person only made that demand to white people but totally ignored people of other races.

This is also the only Pick-n-Pull that I have ever been to where the employees go out to the yard and start chasing people down to screech at them when they simply lower their masks to catch a breath of fresh air while they are 50 feet away from the nearest person.

All the other ones that I have been to just follow the CDC guidelines that say wear it when social distancing is not possible<//text>

Andrew is severely handicapped, and his brother and financial custodian had arranged with the company to make phone payment with the installers while they were on site and working. The problem arose when the installers arrived early, demanding payment before they would begin work, and Andrew couldn't immediately contact his brother to confirm payment. Rather than recognize the unique situation, the installers would not lift a finger to begin work, but left Andrew sitting on the porch, while they left to other jobs. Andrew's brother then spent the rest of the day--on telephone hold--with Empire's impersonal and powerless call centers. Have you ever spent a day on maddening hold with customer service, only to realize that they are powerless to do anything on your behalf? They just give you continuous cliches about how sorry they are for your inconvenience? That was our day with Empire. It was clear throughout the day that Empire's business model is not one tailored to customer service. The lesson for consumers is simple. First, no credible carpet company would demand payment in advance, before inspection of work is completed. Second, no reputable carpet company would employ installers that cannot recognize a unique situation and work within that situation in the customers' interest. Finally, Empire is a company that employs an impersonal call center "barrier," with telephone agents that are powerless to take action and are disconnected with other company departments. I had purchase flooring from them in January of 2019. I had a horrible interaction with them that time and still another one with this time! I called to complain because I had lost a significant amount of money from my job being gone an unexpected 5 days instead of 2 (I was on the phone with customer service several times throughout this job and no one could ever seem to help me). I was hung up on by one teller because I told her I would wait on hold for the manager to get on the phone and she said she needed her line freed up to take other calls. Finally the manager called me back and did nothing for me. I emailed a very long message to their corporate office and they subsidized my cost of installation by $600 due to the money lost in my days of not working unexpectedly. Didn't account for the significant emotional stress I endured through this! However, why could no one at the managerial or general manager level help me at the SD location?? No idea!
Later, July of 2019 I had a house flood which led to some removal of my brand new flooring and needing to be replaced. I did not want to go through Empire, but was forced to because they would not sell me the floor out right and apparently monopolize the flooring industry to some degree, so only they sell the type of floor that they put in my home. <username>Trevor Thomas</username>< Review>
I chose two stars rather than one because the gym is extant; if you're already a 24 member, having some gym space available here is better than having none. But on its own terms, this is the worst gym I've ever trained at. The free weight areas are tiny and poorly stocked, with a limited collection of weights, a single worryingly rickety power rack, a single bench, a characteristically worthless Smith machine, and no space to deadlift. The upstairs area has a collection of early-90s Nautilus machines (that, to the gym's credit, does at least include one cable tower, however janky and over-subscribed). There are no showers and extremely limited locker space. But the space is clean, and the staff seems nice, and again: it exists.<//Review>

<rating>4< /rating>< review>
I'm a member here and it's a little misleading calling it a supersport club because there is no pool or showers. I was told they had to classify the club this way because a major gym just opened on the same block. It has a very relaxed vibe. All the weights, machines and other equipment needed is here. Being classified a supersport club does give you acces to all the other supersport clubs that do have pools in the country. Entry is done through finger scanner and phone number. No cards to get in. The red brick walls feel right and comfortable for the gym. Staff is very friendly and helpful. You have the feeling that the staff knows you and it never feels crowded. It's a comfortable place to get a workout in before or after work. Very large parking garage right next door.</review>

<UserId.>103609840536806013092<//UserId.><Name>El Colombiano< /Name>< time>

<rate>5< /rate>< text>
This is the best hole in the wall restaurant for teriyaki food in Glendale!!! Been coming here for roughly 15 years and will continue to go till their last day. I always get the shrimp chowmein but the chicken and beef is really good too! Their teriyaki sauce is home made and sooo good! What I like about this place is that food is made to order. It's not like Panda Express that sometimes has food sitting for a while. I mean it's not bad once in a blue moon but mitzees is way better especially on the rainy days lol. If your thinking about going but unsure, don't hesitate, pull the trigger. And when you go, make sure to leave a review. Allot of us now a days go by reviews.

When you go, make sure you ask questions just to be sure your not allergic to anything or whatever.

Small plate is $8 and change and large I think $10. Almost everyone, I get the $8 because it's good portions and pretty filling.

Also, it might not look like they have a bathroom but they do. It's all the way to the back and thru the door, you'll see it.

Stop by, you won't regret it, I promise!<//text>

Potential! This is a locals restaurant that could easily blossom into a into one of my go-to's for a great meal with friends and family.  Like most mom & pops, all it needs is a little love and the time needed to grow into its space. <date>1580839154935</date><text>Though there are more than one Pane e Vino restaurantts, this one stands out for its authenticity. Our favorite waiter has worked here for over 20 years, and his accent is still influenced by his native Italian roots. The food is equally authentic, and the menu is quizzically long and diverse - a benefit abandoned long ago by most restaurants driven by a profit requirement.  The wine list features enough domestic wines to satisfy those whose palates are attuned to tthe California style, but the list is still dominated by Italian wines of good quality. If Italian wines are a mystery to you (you're not alone!!) just ask your server for a recommendation once you've made your dining decisions, and he/she will recommend a match made in heaven.<//text></record></dataset><record>

This restaurant obviously panders to a certain crowd. A crowd that looking around is probably retired or close to.
The service was slow but friendly. The bus boys were quick to clear plates but never refilled water.
I had a glass of Prosecco, and would have liked a second one with my main course but was never attended to by the water or service staff.
My friend had the Scallops as an entree they were fragrant in all the wrong ways but apparently palatable to him.
My entree was the Risotto with Seafood and it was bland/plain (probably to cater to older palates) the shrimp was hard and had more bite then most of the clientele and I could not eat much more as it was simply unappetizing. An Entree for 25 dollars and I will probably hunt down a slice of pizza else where on my way home.
This was a major disappointment on all levels.</Text>

< text>
I moved back to SF a few months ago after a 30 year absence, and am finding new favorite restaurants. We were looking for a nice meal after work and decided to drive up Union street and see what we could find. We passed Pane e Vino, and there was a good crowd for a weeknight, so we decided to take chance. We are so happy we did. We have been there three times now, and everything we have ordered was perfect. The service is always friendly and accommodating. The dining room is a bit crowded, but full of life. On our last visit, we found there is a patio out back that is more to our liking. It feels like Italy, it tastes like Italy - dolce far niente!<//text>

5 STARS OK,5.

I TRULY CAN NOT SAY ENOUGH ABOUT THIS PLACE, I HAVE DRIVEN BY SOOOOOO MANY TIMES SAYING

"IM GOING IN ONE DAY."

OK I WASTED A LOT OF TIME NOT DOING SO AND MISSING A DARN GOOD MEAL, good atmosphere, Hometown feel, ( which I miss from my part of Texas,") exceptional service, not good,  EXCEPTIONAL!!!!
The service was so exceptional I honestly cannot tell you who my server was but in the end Mesa (My OPOLIGIES if spelled incorrectly)  is the individual server that picked up my check HOWEVER  one person greeted me at the door, another met me at my table and ask ABOUT drinks, another brought the food to the table, and upon my eating it was almost celebrity Service.

As there was constant attention of do you you need this, do you need that etc..
This day I was multitasking and I was on the phone (witch I hate to do especially while eating) my counterpart could  hear the service  and asked if I was in uniform.  (I was not)  it was just exceptional service The meal was exquisite. The service phenomenal.

Had to wait a bit, but I CLEARLY understand why.
I will start being my team, and club members to this location.

Again MESA I advised you I would add your name to my Review & and done so, You ALL were GREAT...

<text>On a business trip decided to give this place a try due to other reviews. I was not misled. This is a small place, if your heading north on Vineyard and catch the light to tunn on 8th you'll like drive right past. It's right at the corner, don't miss it. inside is nice and friendly and the staff is helpful and attentive. I was recommended the chicken fried steak for breakfast and wanting the best of both worlds I did the diced chicken fried steak omelet. I saved on lunch because I was still stuffed when lunch time rolled around. Everything was well prepared and not over cooked. <userid>114366257779026969049<//userid><username>Dan and Cheree Griffith</username><time>1551987718377</time><Rate>4< /Rate>< review>
Pleasantly surprised! We had been to this site previously under prior ownership  ... it had been a typical 'greasy spoon.' Things have been elevated! Still a bucket load of comfort food on the menu but it's minus the 'greasy' part! We were here at Breakfast time while having our car serviced up the street (at The Auto Shop, a honest-to-goodness HONEST mechanic,  Al Davis). Greeting was very friendly.  Server Brian proved to be a pleasure. We decided to split the Chicken Fried Steak & eggs plate as we had heard that the portion sizes here were quite generous. As our meal arrived, it had already been split in the Kitchen onto two plates and both were visually appealing. The food was fresh and tasty. Even though Brian brought us steak knives, they weren't necessary as we could cut through they protein with our forks. The biscuits & gravy were spot on and the home fries are a winner. Can't wait to try other menu items! We'll surely schedule our next car service accordingly!< /review>
